  * grade_story_1.txt (grade=3.8)
    The plot structure suffers from weak causality and forced connections. The garage sale envelope containing a map to a fisherman's net inside a pyramid creates a contrived scenario. The metaphorical connection between untying knots and overcoming anxiety is heavy-handed. The resolution feels rushed and unearned, with the final triumph lacking sufficient buildup or meaningful obstacles.

  * grade_story_10.txt (grade=3.8)

The connection between the chest's contents and Jarek's journey toward forgiveness is tenuous at best. The narrative feels like a series of statements rather than a developing arc with clear cause-and-effect relationships.

The ending offers no real resolution or transformation beyond what was already stated.

  * grade_story_100.txt (grade=4.8)
